<!-- Admission Counselor -->
<script>
  
(function() {

  
  /*
 #############################
 ## Get Industry for dropdown     
 ##############################
 */ 
   var industry = "Accounting,Arts,Business,Communications/Marketing/Media,Education,Environmental Studies,Finance,Government,Health Professions/Services & Research,Law,Nonprofit/Social Services,Tech/Data & Analytics";

	industry = industry.split(',');
    industry = industry.sort();
    
    //Add default all to list
    $('#industry').append('<option value="" selected="selected">All</option>');
    
    $.each(industry, function(i, v) {
        v = v.trim();
      (v) ? $('#industry').append('<option value="' + v + '">' + v + '</option>') : null;
    });
  
  
  /*
 #############################
 ## Get State for dropdown     
 ##############################
 */ 
   var state = "AK, AL, AR, AS, AZ, CA, CO, CT, DC, DE, FL, GA, GU, HI, IA, ID, IL, IN, KS, KY, LA, MA, MD, ME, MI, MN, MO, MP, MS, MT, NC, ND, NE, NH, NJ, NM, NV, NY, OH, OK, OR, PA, PR, RI, SC, SD, TN, TX, UM, UT, VA, VI, VT, WA, WI, WV, WY, International";

	state = state.split(',');
    //state = state.sort();
    
    //Add default all to list
    $('#state').append('<option value="" selected="selected">All</option>');
    
    $.each(state, function(i, v) {
        v = v.trim();
      (v) ? $('#state').append('<option value="' + v + '">' + v + '</option>') : null;
    });
  
  
  
  /*
 #############################
 ## When search button is clicked        
 ##############################
 */
  
   $('.search').on('click', function() {
       var industry = $('#industry').val();
       var state = $('#state').val();
         
         
       filterSelection(industry,state);
        
     });
  
  
  /*
 #############################
 ## When clear filters button is clicked        
 ##############################
 */
  
   $('.clear').on('click', function() {
     
       //var industry = $('#industry').val();
      // var state = $('#state').val();
          var x,i, count=0;
  x = document.getElementsByClassName("filterAlumni");
    
  for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) { 
    AddClass(x[i], "show");}
     
      $('.no-counselors').text(""); 
     document.getElementById("state").selectedIndex = 0;
     document.getElementById("industry").selectedIndex = 0;


         

        
     });
  

  
  /*
 #############################
 ## Function to loop through  
 ##############################
 */   

function filterSelection(industry,state) {
  var x,i, count=0;
  x = document.getElementsByClassName("filterAlumni");
    
  
  // Add the "show" class and remove from the elements that are not selected 
  for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) { 
     RemoveClass(x[i], "show");
    for (a = 0; a < industry.length; a++) {
       for (b = 0; b < state.length; b++) {
         var filters =  industry[a] + '_' + state[b];
             if (x[i].className.indexOf(filters) > -1){
                 AddClass(x[i], "show");
                 count++;     
             }
       }
    }

  }
  
  /*
 ####################################
 ## Display message if none found     
 ####################################
 */ 
  if (count == 0){
     if (industry){
      industry = "<li><strong>Industry:</strong> " + industry + "</li>";
    }
     if (state){
       state = "<li><strong>State:</strong> " + state + "</li>";
    }
   $('.no-counselors').html("<br/>No Alumni found for:<ul> " + industry + state + "</ul>");    
  }
  else {
    $('.no-counselors').text("");     
  }
}
   

  
  /*
 #############################
 ## Show filtered items    
 ##############################
 */ 
function AddClass(element, name) {
  var i, arr1, arr2;
  arr1 = element.className.split(" ");
  arr2 = name.split(" ");
  for (i = 0; i < arr2.length; i++) {
    if (arr1.indexOf(arr2[i]) == -1) {
      element.className += " " + arr2[i];

    }
  }
  
}  
  
  
  /*
 #############################
 ## Hide filtered Items    
 ##############################
 */ 
function RemoveClass(element, name) {
  var i, arr1, arr2;
  arr1 = element.className.split(" ");
  arr2 = name.split(" ");
  for (i = 0; i < arr2.length; i++) {
    while (arr1.indexOf(arr2[i]) > -1) {
      arr1.splice(arr1.indexOf(arr2[i]), 1);
    }
  }
  element.className = arr1.join(" ");
  
}
     
  })();

</script>
